This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-pantry)
  (:domain house-exploration)

  (:objects
    kitchen pantry east-room west-room corridor - location
    north south east west - direction
  )

  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (door kitchen pantry south)
    (door pantry kitchen north)
    (door kitchen east-room east)
    (door kitchen west-room west)
    (door kitchen corridor north)
    (door-closed kitchen east-room)
    (door-closed kitchen west-room)
    (door-closed kitchen corridor)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
  )

  (:goal
    (at east-room)
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )
  
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous problem file:

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )
  
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-house)
  (:domain house-exploration)

  (:objects
    kitchen pantry backyard room_west - location

    (door room_west kitchen east)
    (door-closed kitchen room_west)
    (door-closed room_west kitchen)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)

Parsed df and pf: 
 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)
